### Round 12: Belgian Grand Prix
*Date: 2017-08-27*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 20: Abu Dhabi Grand Prix
*Date: 2017-11-26*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
